    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">On March 17, 2023, T-Mobile US, Inc. (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline;">Company</span>&#8221;) announced the completion of the previously announced consent solicitations by its wholly-owned subsidiaries
      Sprint LLC (&#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline;">Sprint</span>&#8221;) and Sprint Capital Corporation (&#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline;">SCC</span>&#8221;) (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline;">Consent Solicitations</span>&#8221;) and the receipt, as of March 17, 2023, of the requisite consents to approve the Sprint Indenture Amendments and the SCC Indenture
      Amendments (each as defined below), respectively.</div>

    <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>

    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">On March 17, 2023, Sprint entered into the Ninth Supplemental Indenture (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline;">Sprint Supplemental Indenture</span>&#8221;) by and between Sprint and The Bank of New York Mellon
      Trust Company, N.A. (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline;">Sprint Trustee</span>&#8221;), which amends and supplements the Senior Notes Indenture, dated as of September 11, 2013, by and between Sprint and the Sprint Trustee (as amended and supplemented, the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline;">Sprint Indenture</span>&#8221;).&#160;
      The Sprint Supplemental Indenture effects certain amendments (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline;">Sprint Indenture Amendments</span>&#8221;) to the Sprint Indenture pertaining to Sprint&#8217;s 7.875% Notes due 2023, 7.125% Notes due 2024, 7.625% Notes due 2025 and 7.625% Notes due 2026
      (collectively, the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline;">Sprint Notes</span>&#8221;).&#160; Holders representing 91.30%, 93.32%, 95.92% and 93.96% in aggregate principal amount of Sprint&#8217;s 7.875% Notes due 2023, 7.125% Notes due 2024, 7.625% Notes due 2025 and 7.625% Notes due 2026, respectively,
      consented to the Sprint Indenture Amendments.</div>

    <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>

    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Also on March 17, 2023, SCC entered into the Sixth Supplemental Indenture (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline;">SCC Supplemental Indenture</span>&#8221;) by and among SCC, Sprint Communications LLC (&#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline;">Sprint
        Communications</span>&#8221;) and The Bank of New York Mellon Trust Company, N.A. (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline;">SCC Trustee</span>&#8221;), which amends and supplements the Indenture, dated as of October 1, 1998, by and among SCC, Sprint Communications and the SCC Trustee (as amended
      and supplemented, the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline;">SCC Indenture</span>&#8221;).&#160; The SCC Supplemental Indenture effects certain amendments (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline;">SCC Indenture Amendments</span>&#8221; and together with the Sprint Indenture Amendments, the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline;">Indenture Amendments</span>&#8221;) to the SCC
      Indenture pertaining to SCC&#8217;s 6.875% Notes due 2028 and 8.750% Notes due 2032 (collectively, the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline;">SCC Notes</span>&#8221; and together with the Sprint Notes, the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline;">Notes</span>&#8221;).&#160; Holders representing 88.83% and 94.03% in aggregate principal amount of
      SCC&#8217;s 6.875% Notes due 2028 and 8.750% Notes due 2032, respectively, consented to the SCC Indenture Amendments.</div>

    <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>

    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">The Indenture Amendments are being effected in connection with the Membership Interest Purchase Agreement, dated as of September 6, 2022 (as it may be amended, supplemented
      or modified from time to time, the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline;">Purchase Agreement</span>&#8221;), made by and among Sprint, Sprint Communications and Cogent Infrastructure, Inc. (&#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline;">Cogent</span>&#8221;), pursuant to which Cogent agreed to acquire certain assets and liabilities primarily
      relating to the U.S. long-haul fiber network (including the non-U.S. extensions thereof) of Sprint Communications and its subsidiaries (such assets and liabilities collectively, the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline;">Wireline Business</span>&#8221;) on the terms and subject to the
      conditions set forth in the Purchase Agreement.&#160; The Purchase Agreement provides that, upon the terms and conditions set forth therein, Sprint Communications will undertake a divisive merger and Cogent will purchase from Sprint all of the issued and
      outstanding membership interests of a newly formed Delaware limited liability company resulting from such divisive merger that holds the Wireline Business (such transactions contemplated by the Purchase Agreement, the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline;">Wireline Transaction</span>&#8221;).</div>

    <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>

    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">The Sprint Indenture Amendments amend the Sprint Indenture to expressly provide that the restriction on mergers, consolidations and transfers of all or substantially all
      property and assets of Sprint Communications shall not apply to the Wireline Transaction or certain divisive mergers in connection with or in contemplation of a disposition or other separation of the Wireline Business.&#160; The SCC Indenture Amendments
      amend the SCC Indenture to expressly provide that the restriction on mergers and consolidations of Sprint Communications shall not apply to the Wireline Transaction or certain divisive mergers in connection with or in contemplation of a disposition
      or other separation of the Wireline Business.</div>

    <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>

    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">The Sprint Supplemental Indenture and the SCC Supplemental Indenture each became effective on March 17, 2023 and the Indenture Amendments will become operative upon the
      payment of the applicable consent payments to the paying agent for the benefit of the holders of each series of Sprint Notes and SCC Notes whose consents were validly delivered (and not revoked) at or prior to the expiration of the applicable Consent
      Solicitation in accordance with the terms and conditions applicable to the relevant Consent Solicitation.</div>

    <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><br />
    </div>

    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">The Sprint Supplemental Indenture and the SCC Supplemental Indenture are attached hereto as Exhibits 4.1 and 4.2, respectively.&#160; The foregoing descriptions of the Sprint
      Supplemental Indenture and the SCC Supplemental Indenture are qualified in their entirety by reference to the full text of the Sprint Supplemental Indenture and SCC Supplemental Indenture, respectively, which are incorporated herein by reference.</div>

    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"> <br />

        <div style="text-align: center; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">SIXTH SUPPLEMENTAL INDENTURE</div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;">SIXTH SUPPLEMENTAL INDENTURE (this &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221;),
          dated as of March 17, 2023, among SPRINT CAPITAL CORPORATION, a Delaware corporation (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Company</font>&#8221;), SPRINT COMMUNICATIONS LLC, a Kansas limited liability company (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Guarantor</font>&#8221;), and THE BANK OF NEW YORK MELLON TRUST COMPANY, N.A., as trustee (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Trustee</font>&#8221;).</div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">
        <div style="text-align: center; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">RECITALS OF THE COMPANY</div>
      </div>
      <div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
        </div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">WHEREAS</font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">,
            the Company heretofore executed and delivered to the Trustee: (i)&#160;an indenture, dated as of October&#160;1, 1998, among the Company, the Guarantor and the Trustee (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Base Indenture</font>&#8221;);
            (ii) an Officers&#8217; Certificate, dated as of November&#160;16, 1998, providing for the issuance of $2,500,000,000 aggregate principal amount of 6.875% Notes due 2028 (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">2028 Notes</font>&#8221;);
            (iii) a First Supplemental Indenture, dated as of January&#160;15, 1999, among the Company, the Guarantor and the Trustee (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">First Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221;); (iv) a Second
            Supplemental Indenture, dated as of October&#160;15, 2001, among the Company, the Guarantor and the Trustee (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Second Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221;); (v) Pricing Committee
            Resolutions, dated as of March&#160;14, 2002, providing for the issuance of $2,000,000,000 aggregate principal amount of 8.750% Notes due 2032 (together with the 2028 Notes, the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Subject
              Securities</font>&#8221;); (vi)&#160;a Third Supplemental Indenture, dated as of September&#160;11, 2013, among the Company, the Guarantor, Sprint LLC, a Delaware limited liability company (&#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Sprint</font>&#8221;),
            and the Trustee (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Third Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221;); (vii) a Fourth Supplemental Indenture, dated as of May 18, 2018, among the Company, the Guarantor and the Trustee
            (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Fourth Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221;); and (viii) a Fifth Supplemental Indenture, dated as of April 1, 2020, among the Company, the Guarantor, Sprint, T-Mobile US, Inc., a
            Delaware corporation, T-Mobile USA, Inc., a Delaware corporation, and the Trustee (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Fifth Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221; and together with the Base Indenture, the First
            Supplemental Indenture, the Second Supplemental Indenture, the Third Supplemental Indenture, the Fourth Supplemental Indenture and the above-referenced officers&#8217; certificate and pricing committee resolutions, which, as applicable, govern the
            terms of the Subject Securities, the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Indenture</font>&#8221;);</font></div>
      </div>
      <div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
        </div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">WHEREAS</font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">,
            Section&#160;902 of the Indenture provides, among other things, that the Indenture may be amended or supplemented by a supplemental indenture thereto with the consent of the Holders of not less than a majority in principal amount of all Outstanding
            Securities of each series affected by such supplemental indenture;</font></div>
      </div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
      </div>
      <div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">WHEREAS</font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">,
            pursuant to the terms of the Indenture, the Company desires to amend and supplement or further amend and supplement, as applicable, (1)&#160;Section 101 of Article I of the Indenture; and (2)&#160;Article VIII of the Indenture (together, the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Subject Amendments</font>&#8221;), in each case with respect to the Subject Securities on the terms set forth in the Company&#8217;s Consent Solicitation Statement dated March 13, 2023 (as
            amended to the date hereof, the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Consent Solicitation Statement</font>&#8221;);</font></div>
      </div>
      <div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
        </div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">WHEREAS</font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">,
            the Company solicited, and has received, consents to the Subject Amendments upon the terms and subject to the conditions set forth in the Consent Solicitation Statement from Holders representing at least a majority in aggregate principal amount
            of each series of the outstanding Subject Securities;</font></div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;">&#160;</div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">WHEREAS</font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">,
            for the purposes hereinabove recited, and pursuant to due corporate action, the Company has duly determined to execute and deliver to the Trustee this Supplemental Indenture; and</font></div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;">&#160;</div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">WHEREAS</font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">,
            all conditions and requirements necessary to make this Supplemental Indenture a valid and binding instrument in accordance with its terms have been done and performed, and the execution and delivery hereof have been in all respects duly
            authorized.</font></div>
        <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 48.95pt; color: #000000; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt;"> <br>
          </font></div>
      </div>
      <div class="BRPFPageBreakArea" style="clear: both; margin-top: 10pt; margin-bottom: 10pt;">
        <div class="BRPFPageBreak" style="page-break-after: always;">
          <hr noshade="noshade" style="margin: 4px 0px; width: 100%; border-width: 0; height: 2px; color: #000000; background-color: #000000; clear: both;"></div>
      </div>
      <div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">NOW, THEREFORE</font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">, in consideration of the premises, the covenants and other agreements contained herein and other good and valuable consideration, the sufficiency of which is hereby confirmed, the Company, the Guarantor and the Trustee mutually covenant
            and agree as follows:</font></div>
      </div>
      <div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
        </div>
        <div style="text-align: center; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">ARTICLE ONE</div>
        <div style="text-align: center; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">AMENDMENT TO THE INDENTURE</div>
      </div>
      <div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
        </div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;">Section&#160;1.01. With respect to the Subject Securities, Section 101 of the Indenture is hereby amended by adding the following
          definitions:</div>
      </div>
      <div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
        </div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; margin-left: 54pt; text-indent: 36pt;">&#8220;Purchase Agreement&#8221; means that certain Membership Interest Purchase Agreement, dated as of September 6,
          2022, made by and among Sprint LLC, the Guarantor and Cogent Infrastructure, Inc., as it may be amended, supplemented or modified from time to time.</div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt; margin-left: 54pt; text-indent: 36pt;">&#160;</div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; margin-left: 54pt; text-indent: 36pt;">&#8220;Wireline Business&#8221; means the assets and liabilities primarily relating to the U.S. long-haul fiber network
          (including the non-U.S. extensions thereof) and certain other assets and liabilities of the Guarantor and its subsidiaries, substantially as set forth in the Purchase Agreement.</div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt; margin-left: 54pt; text-indent: 36pt;">&#160;</div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; margin-left: 54pt; text-indent: 36pt;">&#8220;Wireline Divisive Merger&#8221; means a redomestication of the Guarantor to Delaware followed by a divisive merger
          of the Guarantor, in connection with or in contemplation of a divestiture or other separation of all or part of the Wireline Business, as a result of which (i) the Guarantor will survive as a Delaware limited liability company and, immediately
          following such divisive merger, will hold the assets (including, for the avoidance of doubt, equity of subsidiaries) and liabilities held by the Guarantor immediately prior to such divisive merger other than those relating to the applicable
          portion of the Wireline Business contemplated to be divested or separated and (ii) a newly formed limited liability company resulting from such divisive merger will, immediately following such divisive merger, hold the assets (including, for the
          avoidance of doubt, equity of subsidiaries) and liabilities held by the Guarantor immediately prior to such divisive merger relating to the applicable portion of the Wireline Business contemplated to be divested or separated.</div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt; margin-left: 54pt; text-indent: 36pt;">&#160;</div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; margin-left: 54pt; text-indent: 36pt;">&#8220;Wireline Transaction&#8221; means the transactions contemplated by the Purchase Agreement, including the purchase
          and sale of all of the issued and outstanding membership interests of a newly formed Delaware limited liability company resulting from the Wireline Divisive Merger contemplated by the Purchase Agreement that will hold certain assets (including,
          for the avoidance of doubt, equity of subsidiaries) and liabilities relating to the Wireline Business held by the Guarantor immediately prior to such Wireline Divisive Merger.</div>
      </div>
      <div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
        </div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;">Section&#160;1.02. With respect to the Subject Securities, Article VIII of the Indenture is hereby amended by adding the following
          Section 805 at the end thereof:</div>
      </div>
      <div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
        </div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; margin-left: 54pt; text-indent: 36pt;">Section 805.&#160; <font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Wireline Transaction</font>.</div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt; margin-left: 54pt; text-indent: 36pt;">&#160;</div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; margin-left: 54pt; text-indent: 36pt;">For the avoidance of doubt, and notwithstanding any other provision of the Securities or this Indenture, (i)
          neither the Wireline Transaction nor any Wireline Divisive Merger shall be deemed to be a merger or consolidation of the Guarantor and (ii) immediately following any Wireline Divisive Merger, the Guarantor shall be deemed for all purposes of the
          Securities and this Indenture to have continued its existence uninterrupted and in full force and effect and to have remained the &#8220;Guarantor&#8221; for all purposes of the Securities and this Indenture, notwithstanding the occurrence of such Wireline
          Divisive Merger.</div>
        <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 48.95pt; margin-left: 23.05pt; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"> <br>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="BRPFPageBreakArea" style="clear: both; margin-top: 10pt; margin-bottom: 10pt;">
        <div class="BRPFPageBreak" style="page-break-after: always;">
          <hr noshade="noshade" style="margin: 4px 0px; width: 100%; border-width: 0; height: 2px; color: #000000; background-color: #000000; clear: both;"></div>
      </div>
      <div>
        <div style="text-align: center; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">ARTICLE TWO</div>
        <div style="text-align: center; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">MISCELLANEOUS PROVISIONS</div>
      </div>
      <div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
        </div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;">Section&#160;2.01&#160;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';"><u>Effective Date</u></font>. This Supplemental Indenture shall
          become effective immediately upon its execution and delivery by the Company, the Guarantor and the Trustee but the amendments to the Indenture set forth in Article One shall become operative only upon payment of the Consent Payments (as defined
          in the Consent Solicitation Statement) and shall thereafter bind, or inure to the benefit of, every Holder.</div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;">&#160;</div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;">Section&#160;2.02&#160;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';"><u>Effect of Supplemental Indenture; Conflicts with Indenture</u></font>.
          This Supplemental Indenture is executed by the Company, the Guarantor and the Trustee upon the Company&#8217;s request, pursuant to the provisions of the Indenture, and the terms and conditions hereof shall be deemed to be part of the Indenture for all
          purposes. The Indenture, as amended and supplemented by this Supplemental Indenture, is in all respects hereby adopted, ratified and confirmed. Notwithstanding the foregoing, to the extent that any of the terms of this Supplemental Indenture are
          inconsistent with, or conflict with, the terms of the Indenture, the terms of this Supplemental Indenture shall govern.</div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;">&#160;</div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;">Section&#160;2.03&#160;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';"><u>Counterparts</u></font>. This Supplemental Indenture may be
          executed in counterparts, each of which shall be an original, but such counterparts shall together constitute but one and the same instrument. Exchange of signature pages to this Supplemental Indenture by facsimile or electronic transmission
          shall constitute effective execution and delivery of this Supplemental Indenture.</div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;">&#160;</div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;">Section&#160;2.04&#160;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';"><u>Trustee</u></font>. The Company, by its signature hereto,
          authorizes and directs the Trustee to execute this Supplemental Indenture. In its execution hereof and performance hereunder, the Trustee shall have all of the rights, protections, immunities and indemnities afforded to it under the Indenture.
          The Trustee assumes no responsibility for the correctness of the recitals herein contained, which shall be taken as the statements of the Company and the Guarantor. The Trustee makes no representations and shall have no responsibility as to the
          validity or sufficiency of this Supplemental Indenture or the due authorization and execution hereof by the Company and the Guarantor.</div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;">&#160;</div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;">Section&#160;2.05&#160;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';"><u>Headings</u></font>. The Article and Section headings contained
          herein are for convenience only and shall not affect the construction of this Supplemental Indenture.</div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;">&#160;</div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;">Section&#160;2.06&#160;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';"><u>Governing Law</u></font>. This Supplemental Indenture shall be
          governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of the State of New York.</div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;">&#160;</div>
        <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 54pt;">Section&#160;2.07&#160;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';"><u>Capitalized Terms</u></font>. Capitalized terms used herein
          without definition shall have the meanings assigned to them in the Indenture.</div>
      </div>
      <div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
        </div>

          <div style="text-align: center; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">NINTH SUPPLEMENTAL INDENTURE</div>
        </div>
        <div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
          </div>
          <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 36pt;">NINTH SUPPLEMENTAL INDENTURE (this &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Supplemental
              Indenture</font>&#8221;), dated as of March 17, 2023, between SPRINT LLC, a Delaware limited liability company (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Company</font>&#8221;), and THE BANK OF NEW YORK MELLON TRUST
            COMPANY, N.A., as trustee (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Trustee</font>&#8221;).</div>
        </div>
        <div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
          </div>
          <div style="text-align: center; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">RECITALS OF THE COMPANY</div>
        </div>
        <div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
          </div>
          <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 36pt; color: #000000; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">WHEREAS</font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">,
              the Company and the Trustee have duly executed and delivered that certain Senior Notes Indenture, dated as of September 11, 2013 (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Original</font>&#160;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Indenture</font>&#8221;) between the Company and the Trustee, as amended and supplemented by the Sixth Supplemental Indenture, dated as of May 14, 2018 (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Sixth Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221;), between the Company and the Trustee, and the Eighth Supplemental Indenture, dated as of April 1, 2020 (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Eighth
                Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221;), among the Company, Sprint Communications LLC, a Kansas limited liability company (&#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Sprint Communications</font>&#8221;), T-Mobile US, Inc., a
              Delaware corporation, T-Mobile USA, Inc., a Delaware corporation, and the Trustee (the Original Indenture, as amended and supplemented by the Sixth Supplemental Indenture and the Eighth Supplemental Indenture, the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Base Indenture</font>&#8221;), providing for the issuance from time to time of unsecured debentures, notes or other evidences of indebtedness, to be issued in one or more series (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Securities</font>&#8221;);</font></div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
          <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 36pt; color: #000000; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">WHEREAS</font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">,
              the Company, Sprint Communications and the Trustee have duly executed and delivered the (i) Second Supplemental Indenture, dated as of September 11, 2013, to the Original Indenture, pursuant to which $4,250,000,000 aggregate principal amount
              of 7.875% Notes due 2023 (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">2023 Notes</font>&#8221;) were issued and are outstanding on the date hereof (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Second


                Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221;), (ii) Third Supplemental Indenture, dated as of December 12, 2013, to the Original Indenture, pursuant to which $2,500,000,000 aggregate principal amount of 7.125% Notes due 2024 (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">2024 Notes</font>&#8221;) were issued and are outstanding on the date hereof (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Third Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221;),

              (iii) Fourth Supplemental Indenture, dated as of February 24, 2015, to the Original Indenture, pursuant to which $1,500,000,000 aggregate principal amount of 7.625% Notes due 2025 (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">2025 Notes</font>&#8221;) were issued and are outstanding on the date hereof (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Fourth Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221;), and (iv) Fifth Supplemental Indenture, dated as
              of February 22, 2018, to the Original Indenture, pursuant to which $1,500,000,000 aggregate principal amount of 7.625% Notes due 2026 (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">2026 Notes</font>&#8221; and, collectively
              with the 2023 Notes, the 2024 Notes and the 2025 Notes, the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Subject Securities</font>&#8221;) were issued and are outstanding on the date hereof (the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Fifth Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221; and, collectively with the Second Supplemental Indenture, the Third Supplemental Indenture and the Fourth Supplemental Indenture, the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Subject Supplemental Indentures</font>&#8221; and the Base Indenture as amended and supplemented by the Subject Supplemental Indentures, the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Indenture</font>&#8221;), which, as applicable, govern the terms of the Subject Securities;</font></div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
          <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 36pt; color: #000000; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">WHEREAS</font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">,
              Section 902 of the Indenture provides, among other things, that the Indenture, as amended and supplemented by the Subject Supplemental Indentures, may be amended or supplemented by a supplemental indenture thereto with the consent of the
              Holders of not less than a majority in principal amount of all Outstanding Securities affected by such supplemental indenture;</font></div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
          <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 36pt; color: #000000; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">WHEREAS</font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">,
              pursuant to the terms of the Indenture, the Company desires to amend and supplement or further amend and supplement, as applicable, (1) Section 101 of the Base Indenture; and (2) Article VIII of the Base Indenture (collectively, the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Subject Amendments</font>&#8221;), in each case on the terms set forth in the Company&#8217;s Consent Solicitation Statement dated March 13, 2023 (as amended to the date hereof, the &#8220;<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-style: italic;">Consent Solicitation Statement</font>&#8221;);</font></div>
          <font style="font-size: 10pt;"> </font>
          <div>
            <div style="text-align: center; color: #000000; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"> <br>
            </div>
          </div>
          <font style="font-size: 10pt;"> </font> </div>
        <div style="clear: both; margin-top: 10pt; margin-bottom: 10pt;" class="BRPFPageBreakArea">
          <div style="page-break-after: always;" class="BRPFPageBreak">
            <hr noshade="noshade" style="margin: 4px 0px; width: 100%; border-width: 0; height: 2px; color: #000000; background-color: #000000; clear: both;"></div>
        </div>
        <div>
          <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 36pt; color: #000000; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">WHEREAS</font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">,
              the Company solicited, and has received, consents to the Subject Amendments upon the terms and subject to the conditions set forth in the Consent Solicitation Statement from Holders representing at least a majority in aggregate principal
              amount of each series of the outstanding Subject Securities;</font></div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
          <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 36pt; color: #000000; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">WHEREAS</font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">,
              for the purposes hereinabove recited, and pursuant to due corporate action, the Company has duly determined to execute and deliver to the Trustee this Supplemental Indenture; and</font></div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
          <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 36pt; color: #000000; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">WHEREAS</font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">,
              all conditions and requirements necessary to make this Supplemental Indenture a valid and binding instrument in accordance with its terms have been done and performed, and the execution and delivery hereof have been in all respects duly
              authorized.</font></div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
          <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 36pt; color: #000000; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">NOW, THEREFORE</font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">, in consideration of the premises, the covenants and other agreements contained herein and other good and valuable consideration, the sufficiency of which is hereby confirmed, the Company and the Trustee mutually covenant and agree as
              follows:</font></div>
        </div>
        <div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
          </div>
          <div style="text-align: center; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">ARTICLE ONE</div>
        </div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;">
          <div style="text-align: center; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">AMENDMENT TO THE BASE INDENTURE</div>
        </div>
        <div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
          </div>
          <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 36pt; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Section 1.01. With respect to the Subject Securities, Section 101 of the Indenture is hereby amended by adding the following
            definitions:</div>
        </div>
        <div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
          </div>
          <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; margin-left: 36pt; text-indent: 36pt;">&#8220;Purchase Agreement&#8221; means that certain Membership Interest Purchase Agreement, dated as of
            September 6, 2022, made by and among the Company, the Guarantor and Cogent Infrastructure, Inc., as it may be amended, supplemented or modified from time to time.</div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt; margin-left: 36pt; text-indent: 36pt;">&#160;</div>
          <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; margin-left: 36pt; text-indent: 36pt;">&#8220;Wireline Business&#8221; means the assets and liabilities primarily relating to the U.S. long-haul
            fiber network (including the non-U.S. extensions thereof) and certain other assets and liabilities of the Guarantor and its subsidiaries, substantially as set forth in the Purchase Agreement.</div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt; margin-left: 36pt; text-indent: 36pt;">&#160;</div>
          <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; margin-left: 36pt; text-indent: 36pt;">&#8220;Wireline Divisive Merger&#8221; means a redomestication of the Guarantor to Delaware followed by a
            divisive merger of the Guarantor, in connection with or in contemplation of a divestiture or other separation of all or part of the Wireline Business, as a result of which (i) the Guarantor will survive as a Delaware limited liability company
            and, immediately following such divisive merger, will hold the assets (including, for the avoidance of doubt, equity of subsidiaries) and liabilities held by the Guarantor immediately prior to such divisive merger other than those relating to
            the applicable portion of the Wireline Business contemplated to be divested or separated and (ii) a newly formed limited liability company resulting from such divisive merger will, immediately following such divisive merger, hold the assets
            (including, for the avoidance of doubt, equity of subsidiaries) and liabilities held by the Guarantor immediately prior to such divisive merger relating to the applicable portion of the Wireline Business contemplated to be divested or
            separated.</div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt; margin-left: 36pt; text-indent: 36pt;">&#160;</div>
          <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; margin-left: 36pt; text-indent: 36pt;">&#8220;Wireline Transaction&#8221; means the transactions contemplated by the Purchase Agreement, including
            the purchase and sale of all of the issued and outstanding membership interests of a newly formed Delaware limited liability company resulting from the Wireline Divisive Merger contemplated by the Purchase Agreement that will hold certain
            assets (including, for the avoidance of doubt, equity of subsidiaries) and liabilities relating to the Wireline Business held by the Guarantor immediately prior to such Wireline Divisive Merger.</div>
          <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 36pt; margin-left: 24.5pt; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"> <br>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; margin-top: 10pt; margin-bottom: 10pt;" class="BRPFPageBreakArea">
          <div style="page-break-after: always;" class="BRPFPageBreak">
            <hr noshade="noshade" style="margin: 4px 0px; width: 100%; border-width: 0; height: 2px; color: #000000; background-color: #000000; clear: both;"></div>
        </div>
        <div>
          <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 36pt;">Section 1.02. With respect to the Subject Securities, Article VIII of the Indenture is hereby amended by adding the
            following Section 805 at the end thereof:</div>
        </div>
        <div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
          </div>
          <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 36pt; margin-left: 36pt; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Section 805.&#160; <font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';"><u>Wireline Transaction</u></font>.</div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
          <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 36pt; margin-left: 36pt; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">For the avoidance of doubt, and notwithstanding any other provision of the Securities or this Indenture,
            (i) neither the Wireline Transaction nor any Wireline Divisive Merger shall be deemed to be (A) a merger or consolidation of the Guarantor, (B) a conveyance, transfer or lease of all or substantially all of the properties and assets of the
            Guarantor or (C) a conveyance, transfer or lease of the properties and assets of the Guarantor substantially as an entirety and (ii) immediately following any Wireline Divisive Merger, the Guarantor shall be deemed for all purposes of the
            Securities and this Indenture to have continued its existence uninterrupted and in full force and effect and to have remained the &#8220;Guarantor&#8221; for all purposes of the Securities and this Indenture, notwithstanding the occurrence of such Wireline
            Divisive Merger.</div>
        </div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
        </div>
        <div>
          <div style="text-align: center; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">ARTICLE TWO</div>
          <div style="text-align: center; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">MISCELLANEOUS PROVISIONS</div>
        </div>
        <div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
          </div>
          <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 36pt;">Section 2.01 <font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';"><u>Effective Date</u></font>. This
            Supplemental Indenture shall become effective immediately upon its execution and delivery by the Company and the Trustee but the amendments to the Indenture set forth in Article One shall become operative only upon payment of the Consent
            Payments (as defined in the Consent Solicitation Statement) and shall thereafter bind, or inure to the benefit of, every Holder.</div>
        </div>
        <div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
          </div>
          <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 36pt; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Section 2.02 <font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';"><u>Effect of Supplemental Indenture; Conflicts with Indenture</u></font>.
            This Supplemental Indenture is executed by the Company and the Trustee upon the Company&#8217;s request, pursuant to the provisions of the Indenture, and the terms and conditions hereof shall be deemed to be part of the Indenture for all purposes.
            The Indenture, as amended and supplemented by this Supplemental Indenture, is in all respects hereby adopted, ratified and confirmed. Notwithstanding the foregoing, to the extent that any of the terms of this Supplemental Indenture are
            inconsistent with, or conflict with, the terms of the Indenture, the terms of this Supplemental Indenture shall govern.</div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
          <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 36pt; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Section 2.03 <font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';"><u>Counterparts</u></font>. This Supplemental Indenture may be
            executed in counterparts, each of which shall be an original, but such counterparts shall together constitute but one and the same instrument. Exchange of signature pages to this Supplemental Indenture by facsimile or electronic transmission
            shall constitute effective execution and delivery of this Supplemental Indenture.</div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
          <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 36pt; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Section 2.04 <font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';"><u>Trustee</u></font>. The Company, by its signature hereto,
            authorizes and directs the Trustee to execute this Supplemental Indenture. In its execution hereof and performance hereunder, the Trustee shall have all of the rights, protections, immunities and indemnities afforded to it under the Indenture.
            The Trustee assumes no responsibility for the correctness of the recitals herein contained, which shall be taken as the statements of the Company. The Trustee makes no representations and shall have no responsibility as to the validity or
            sufficiency of this Supplemental Indenture or the due authorization and execution hereof by the Company.</div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
          <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 36pt; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Section 2.05 <font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';"><u>Headings</u></font>. The Article and Section headings contained
            herein are for convenience only and shall not affect the construction of this Supplemental Indenture.</div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
          <div style="text-align: left; text-indent: 36pt; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Section 2.06 <font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';"><u>Governing Law</u></font>. This Supplemental Indenture shall be
            governed by and construed in accordance with the laws of the State of New York.</div>
        </div>
        <div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
          </div>
          <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 36pt;">Section 2.07 <font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';"><u>Capitalized Terms</u></font>. Capitalized
            terms used herein without definition shall have the meanings assigned to them in the Indenture.</div>
        </div>
        <div>
          <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>

<body bgcolor="#ffffff" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; text-align: left; color: #000000;">
  <font style="font-size: 10pt;"> </font>
  <hr noshade="noshade" align="center" style="height: 4px; color: #000000; background-color: #000000; text-align: center; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; border: none;">
  <div>
    <div style="text-align: right; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">Exhibit 99.1</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="text-align: center; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">T-Mobile Announces Successful Consent Solicitations</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">March 17, 2023</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"> <br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">BELLEVUE, Wash.&#8212;(BUSINESS WIRE)&#8212;T-Mobile US, Inc. (NASDAQ: TMUS)<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">&#160;</font>(&#8220;T-Mobile&#8221;) announced today the
      expiration, on March 17, 2023, and results of the consent solicitations by its wholly-owned subsidiaries Sprint LLC (&#8220;Sprint&#8221;) (the &#8220;Sprint Consent Solicitation&#8221;) and Sprint Capital Corporation (&#8220;SCC&#8221;) (the &#8220;SCC Consent Solicitation,&#8221; and together
      with the Sprint Consent Solicitation, the &#8220;Consent Solicitations&#8221;). Sprint received the consents necessary to effect certain amendments to the senior notes indenture, dated as of September 11, 2013 (as supplemented and amended, the &#8220;Sprint
      Indenture&#8221;), governing Sprint&#8217;s 7.875% Notes due 2023 (the &#8220;2023 Notes&#8221;), 7.125% Notes due 2024 (the &#8220;2024 Notes&#8221;), 7.625% Notes due 2025 (the &#8220;2025 Notes&#8221;) and 7.625% Notes due 2026 (the &#8220;2026 Notes,&#8221; and together with the 2023 Notes, the 2024 Notes
      and the 2025 Notes, the &#8220;Sprint Notes&#8221;). SCC received the consents necessary to effect certain amendments to the indenture, dated as of October 1, 1998 (as supplemented and amended, the &#8220;SCC Indenture&#8221;), governing SCC&#8217;s 6.875% Notes due 2028 (the
      &#8220;2028 Notes&#8221;) and 8.750% Notes due 2032 (the &#8220;2032 Notes,&#8221; and together with the 2028 Notes, the &#8220;SCC Notes,&#8221; and together with the Sprint Notes, the &#8220;Notes&#8221;).</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">The Consent Solicitations were conducted in connection with the Membership Interest Purchase Agreement, dated as of September 6, 2022 (as it may be amended, supplemented or
      modified from time to time, the &#8220;Purchase Agreement&#8221;), made by and among Sprint, Sprint Communications LLC (&#8220;Sprint Communications&#8221;) and Cogent Infrastructure, Inc. (&#8220;Cogent&#8221;), pursuant to which Cogent agreed to acquire certain assets and liabilities
      primarily relating to the U.S. long-haul fiber network (including the non-U.S. extensions thereof) of Sprint Communications and its subsidiaries (such assets and liabilities collectively, the &#8220;Wireline Business&#8221;) on the terms and subject to the
      conditions set forth in the Purchase Agreement.&#160; The Purchase Agreement provides that, upon the terms and conditions set forth therein, Sprint Communications will undertake a divisive merger and Cogent will purchase from Sprint all of the issued and
      outstanding membership interests of a newly formed Delaware limited liability company resulting from such divisive merger that holds the Wireline Business (the transactions contemplated by the Purchase Agreement, the &#8220;Wireline Transaction&#8221;).</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">Sprint Consent Solicitation</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Upon the terms and subject to the conditions described in Sprint&#8217;s Consent Solicitation Statement, dated March 13, 2023 (the &#8220;Sprint Solicitation Statement&#8221;), Sprint
      solicited consents from registered holders of the Sprint Notes to expressly provide that the restriction on mergers, consolidations and transfers of all or substantially all property and assets of Sprint Communications shall not apply to the Wireline
      Transaction or certain divisive mergers in connection with or in contemplation of a disposition or other separation of the Wireline Business (such amendments, the &#8220;Sprint Amendments&#8221;).</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">In conjunction with receiving the requisite consents, on March 17, 2023, Sprint and The Bank of New York Mellon Trust Company, N.A., as trustee (the &#8220;Sprint Trustee&#8221;),
      executed and delivered the ninth supplemental indenture (the &#8220;Ninth Supplemental Indenture&#8221;) to the Sprint Indenture (such time, the &#8220;Sprint Effective Time&#8221;), pursuant to which, with respect to each series of Sprint Notes, the Sprint Amendments will
      become operative upon the payment of the Consent Payments (as defined in the Sprint Solicitation Statement) in accordance with the terms and conditions set forth in the Sprint Solicitation Statement. Except for the Sprint Amendments, all of the
      existing terms of the Sprint Notes and the Sprint Indenture will remain unchanged.</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Sprint will pay to D.F. King &amp; Co., Inc. (the &#8220;Tabulation and Payment Agent&#8221;) a cash payment of $1.00 per $1,000 in principal amount of Sprint Notes set forth in the
      table below for the benefit of the holders of each series of Sprint Notes whose consents were validly delivered (and not revoked) at or prior to the expiration of the Sprint Consent Solicitation, upon the terms and subject to the conditions described
      in the Sprint Solicitation Statement. Payment will be made promptly after the date hereof and is expected to be made on March 20<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">, 2023.</font></div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> <br>
      </font></div>

    </div>

    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">SCC Consent Solicitation</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Upon the terms and subject to the conditions described in SCC&#8217;s Consent Solicitation Statement, dated March 13, 2023 (the &#8220;SCC Solicitation Statement&#8221;), SCC solicited
      consents from registered holders of the SCC Notes to expressly provide that the restriction on mergers and consolidations of Sprint Communications shall not apply to the Wireline Transaction or certain divisive mergers in connection with or in
      contemplation of a disposition or other separation of the Wireline Business (such amendments, the &#8220;SCC Amendments&#8221;).</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">In conjunction with receiving the requisite consents, on March 17, 2023, SCC, Sprint Communications and The Bank of New York Mellon Trust Company, N.A., as trustee (the
      &#8220;SCC Trustee&#8221;), executed and delivered the sixth supplemental indenture (the &#8220;Sixth Supplemental Indenture&#8221;) to the SCC Indenture (such time, the &#8220;SCC Effective Time&#8221;), pursuant to which, with respect to each series of SCC Notes, the SCC Amendments
      will become operative upon the payment of the Consent Payments (as defined in the SCC Solicitation Statement) in accordance with the terms and conditions set forth in the SCC Solicitation Statement. Except for the SCC Amendments, all of the existing
      terms of the SCC Notes and the SCC Indenture will remain unchanged.</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">SCC will pay to the Tabulation and Payment Agent a cash payment of $1.00 per $1,000 in principal amount of SCC Notes set forth in the table below for the benefit of the
      holders of each series of SCC Notes whose consents were validly delivered (and not revoked) at or prior to the expiration of the SCC Consent Solicitation, upon the terms and subject to the conditions described in the SCC Solicitation Statement.
      Payment will be made promptly after the date hereof and is expected to be made on March 20<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">, 2023.</font></div>

      announcement is also not a solicitation of consents with respect to the Proposed Amendments or any securities. The solicitation of consents by Sprint was made only pursuant to the Sprint Solicitation Statement, and the solicitation of consents by SCC
      was made only pursuant to the SCC Solicitation Statement.</div>

    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">About T-Mobile</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">T-Mobile US, Inc. (NASDAQ: TMUS) is America&#8217;s supercharged Un-carrier, delivering an advanced 4G LTE and transformative nationwide 5G network that will offer reliable
      connectivity for all. T-Mobile&#8217;s customers benefit from its unmatched combination of value and quality, unwavering obsession with offering them the best possible service experience and undisputable drive for disruption that creates competition and
      innovation in wireless and beyond. Based in Bellevue, Wash., T-Mobile provides services through its subsidiaries and operates its flagship brands, T-Mobile and Metro by T-Mobile.</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>

      contained in this press release (whether as a result of new information, future events or otherwise), except as required by applicable law.</div>
